### PR_ATTACH_CONTENT_ID {#PR-ATTACH-CONTENT-ID}
```
public static final long PR_ATTACH_CONTENT_ID
```


Contains the content identification header of a MIME message attachment. This property is used for MHTML support.

--------------------

It can be used to distinguish between inline attachments such as signature images and normal attached files. If Attachment has this property, then it is an embedded image.

### PR_ATTACH_CONTENT_ID_A {#PR-ATTACH-CONTENT-ID-A}
```
public static final long PR_ATTACH_CONTENT_ID_A
```


Contains the content identification header of a MIME message attachment. This property is used for MHTML support. Non-UNICODE compilation.

--------------------

It can be used to distinguish between inline attachments such as signature images and normal attached files. If Attachment has this property, then it is an embedded image.

### PR_ATTACH_CONTENT_ID_W {#PR-ATTACH-CONTENT-ID-W}
```
public static final long PR_ATTACH_CONTENT_ID_W
```


Contains the content identification header of a MIME message attachment. This property is used for MHTML support. UNICODE compilation.

--------------------

It can be used to distinguish between inline attachments such as signature images and normal attached files. If Attachment has this property, then it is an embedded image.
